001|# Video Verification Claims Web App PRD
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Vite, React, MUI, Tailwind CSS
006|- **Project Name**: video_verification_claims_web_app

008|## 2. Product Definition
009|### Product Goals
010|1. Implement a secure and user-friendly claims submission process with Google authentication.
011|2. Provide a comprehensive claims dashboard for users to track their claims status.
012|
013|### User Stories
014|1. As a user, I want to log in using my Google account so that I can securely access my claims.
015|2. As a claims adjuster, I want to view all submitted claims in a dashboard so that I can manage and verify them efficiently.
016|3. As a user, I want to initiate a video call for claims verification so that I can provide real-time evidence.
017|4. As a user, I want to fill out a multi-step claim form so that I can provide detailed information about my claim.
018|5. As a user, I want to receive email notifications about my claim status so that I am always informed.
019|
020|### Competitive Analysis
021|1. **Product A**
022|   - **Pros**: User-friendly interface, robust security features.
023|   - **Cons**: Limited customization options.
024|2. **Product B**
025|   - **Pros**: Comprehensive dashboard, excellent customer support.
026|   - **Cons**: High pricing model.
027|3. **Product C**
028|   - **Pros**: Integrates well with third-party services, good performance.
029|   - **Cons**: Steep learning curve for new users.
030|4. **Product D**
031|   - **Pros**: Strong video conferencing capabilities, mobile-friendly.
032|   - **Cons**: Occasional bugs in the system.
033|5. **Product E**
034|   - **Pros**: Affordable pricing, easy to set up.
035|   - **Cons**: Lacks advanced features.
036|
037|### Technical Specifications
038|#### Requirements Analysis
039|- **Google Authentication**: Implement OAuth 2.0 for secure user login.
040|- **Claims Dashboard**: A user-friendly interface to view and manage claims.
041|- **Video Calls**: Integrate Jitsi Meet for real-time video communication.
042|- **Geo-location Capture**: Use HTML5 Geolocation API to capture user location.
043|- **Media Storage**: Utilize AWS S3 for storing media files securely.
044|- **Multi-step Claim Forms**: Design forms that guide users through the claims process.
045|- **PDF Report Generation**: Generate downloadable PDF reports for claims.
046|- **Email Notifications**: Use FastAPI or AWS SES for sending email updates.
047|

050|  - Google Authentication
051|  - Claims Dashboard

001|# Video Verification Claims Web App PRD
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Vite, React, MUI, Tailwind CSS
006|- **Project Name**: video_verification_claims_web_app
007|
008|## 2. Product Definition
009|### Product Goals
010|1. Implement a secure and user-friendly claims submission process with Google authentication.
011|2. Provide a comprehensive claims dashboard for users to track their claims status.
012|
013|### User Stories
014|1. As a user, I want to log in using my Google account so that I can securely access my claims.
015|2. As a claims adjuster, I want to view all submitted claims in a dashboard so that I can manage and verify them efficiently.
016|3. As a user, I want to initiate a video call for claims verification so that I can provide real-time evidence.
017|4. As a user, I want to fill out a multi-step claim form so that I can provide detailed information about my claim.
018|5. As a user, I want to receive email notifications about my claim status so that I am always informed.
019|
020|### Competitive Analysis
021|1. **Product A**
022|   - **Pros**: User-friendly interface, robust security features.
023|   - **Cons**: Limited customization options.
024|2. **Product B**
025|   - **Pros**: Comprehensive dashboard, excellent customer support.
026|   - **Cons**: High pricing model.
027|3. **Product C**
028|   - **Pros**: Integrates well with third-party services, good performance.
029|   - **Cons**: Steep learning curve for new users.
030|4. **Product D**
031|   - **Pros**: Strong video conferencing capabilities, mobile-friendly.
032|   - **Cons**: Occasional bugs in the system.
033|5. **Product E**
034|   - **Pros**: Affordable pricing, easy to set up.
035|   - **Cons**: Lacks advanced features.
036|
037|### Technical Specifications
038|#### Requirements Analysis
039|- **Google Authentication**: Implement OAuth 2.0 for secure user login.
040|- **Claims Dashboard**: A user-friendly interface to view and manage claims.
041|- **Video Calls**: Integrate Jitsi Meet for real-time video communication.
042|- **Geo-location Capture**: Use HTML5 Geolocation API to capture user location.
043|- **Media Storage**: Utilize AWS S3 for storing media files securely.
044|- **Multi-step Claim Forms**: Design forms that guide users through the claims process.
045|- **PDF Report Generation**: Generate downloadable PDF reports for claims.
046|- **Email Notifications**: Use FastAPI or AWS SES for sending email updates.
047|
048|#### Requirements Pool
049|- **P0 (Must-have)**:
050|  - Google Authentication
051|  - Claims Dashboard
052|  - Video Calls
053|  - Multi-step Claim Forms
054|- **P1 (Should-have)**:
055|  - Geo-location Capture
056|  - Media Storage in AWS S3
057|  - PDF Report Generation
058|- **P2 (Nice-to-have)**:
059|  - Email Notifications
060|
061|#### UI Design Draft
062|- **Login Page**: A simple interface for Google authentication with a prominent login button.
063|- **Claims Dashboard**: A grid layout displaying all claims with status indicators and action buttons for each claim.
064|- **Video Call Interface**: A full-screen layout for Jitsi Meet with options to mute, end call, and share screen.
065|- **Claim Form**: A multi-step form with progress indicators, input fields for user information, and file upload options.
066|- **PDF Report Page**: A layout for displaying generated reports with download options.
067|3. Enable real-time video calls for claims verification using Jitsi Meet.

001|# Video Verification Claims Web App PRD
002|
003|## 1. Language & Project Info
004|- **Language**: English
005|- **Programming Language**: Vite, React, MUI, Tailwind CSS
006|- **Project Name**: video_verification_claims_web_app
007|
008|## 2. Product Definition
009|### Product Goals
010|1. Implement a secure and user-friendly claims submission process with Google authentication.
011|2. Provide a comprehensive claims dashboard for users to track their claims status.
012|
013|### User Stories
014|1. As a user, I want to log in using my Google account so that I can securely access my claims.
015|2. As a claims adjuster, I want to view all submitted claims in a dashboard so that I can manage and verify them efficiently.
016|3. As a user, I want to initiate a video call for claims verification so that I can provide real-time evidence.
017|4. As a user, I want to fill out a multi-step claim form so that I can provide detailed information about my claim.
018|5. As a user, I want to receive email notifications about my claim status so that I am always informed.
019|
020|### Competitive Analysis
021|1. **Product A**
022|   - **Pros**: User-friendly interface, robust security features.
023|   - **Cons**: Limited customization options.
024|2. **Product B**
025|   - **Pros**: Comprehensive dashboard, excellent customer support.
026|   - **Cons**: High pricing model.
027|3. **Product C**
028|   - **Pros**: Integrates well with third-party services, good performance.
029|   - **Cons**: Steep learning curve for new users.
030|4. **Product D**
031|   - **Pros**: Strong video conferencing capabilities, mobile-friendly.
032|   - **Cons**: Occasional bugs in the system.
033|5. **Product E**
034|   - **Pros**: Affordable pricing, easy to set up.
035|   - **Cons**: Lacks advanced features.
036|

038|#### Requirements Analysis
039|- **Google Authentication**: Implement OAuth 2.0 for secure user login.
040|- **Claims Dashboard**: A user-friendly interface to view and manage claims.
041|- **Video Calls**: Integrate Jitsi Meet for real-time video communication.
042|- **Geo-location Capture**: Use HTML5 Geolocation API to capture user location.
043|- **Media Storage**: Utilize AWS S3 for storing media files securely.
044|- **Multi-step Claim Forms**: Design forms that guide users through the claims process.
045|- **PDF Report Generation**: Generate downloadable PDF reports for claims.
046|- **Email Notifications**: Use FastAPI or AWS SES for sending email updates.
047|

050|  - Google Authentication

053|  - Multi-step Claim Forms
